//===== TERMUXFILE: --max-steps =====


//===== TERMUXFILE: scripts/build_runner.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
#
# build_runner.sh — Autonomous-safe version
#
# Build status contract:
#   /sdcard/ai-automation/build_status.txt    → "SUCCESS" or "FAILURE"
#   /sdcard/ai-automation/build_complete.flag → touched last, always
#
# Android reads build_status.txt for result. Folder existence never used.

set -euo pipefail

REPO_DIR="/data/data/com.termux/files/home/jarvis"
BASE_DIR="/sdcard/ai-automation"
AI_OUTPUT="$BASE_DIR/ai-output.txt"
DOWNLOAD_DIR="/sdcard/Download"
COMPLETE_FLAG="$BASE_DIR/build_complete.flag"
ASSEMBLED_FLAG="$BASE_DIR/downloads_assembled.flag"
SNAPSHOT_FILE="$BASE_DIR/download_snapshot.txt"
STATUS_FILE="$BASE_DIR/build_status.txt"
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
ERROR_LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/build_error_logs"

mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
exec >> "$LOG_DIR/build_runner.log" 2>&1

echo ""
echo "=== build_runner.sh START $(date) args=${*:-none} ==="

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# MODE: snapshot
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [[ "${1:-}" == "--snapshot" ]]; then
    echo "[snapshot] Recording existing files"
    rm -f "$SNAPSHOT_FILE"
    find "$DOWNLOAD_DIR" -maxdepth 1 -type f -exec basename {} \; \
        > "$SNAPSHOT_FILE" 2>/dev/null || true
    echo "[snapshot] Done"
    exit 0
fi

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# MODE: assemble downloaded files
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [[ "${1:-}" == "--assemble-downloads" ]]; then
    echo "[assemble] Starting"

    declare -A BEFORE
    if [[ -f "$SNAPSHOT_FILE" ]]; then
        while IFS= read -r name; do
            BEFORE["$name"]=1
        done < "$SNAPSHOT_FILE"
    fi

    CODE_EXTS="kt java py txt xml json gradle kts sh cpp c h ts js md"
    NEW_FILES=()
    DEADLINE=$(( $(date +%s) + 30 ))

    while (( $(date +%s) < DEADLINE )); do
        while IFS= read -r -d '' f; do
            NAME=$(basename "$f")
            EXT="${NAME##*.}"
            if [[ -z "${BEFORE[$NAME]+_}" ]] && \
               [[ -s "$f" ]] && \
               echo "$CODE_EXTS" | grep -qw "$EXT"; then
                NEW_FILES+=("$f")
            fi
        done < <(find "$DOWNLOAD_DIR" -maxdepth 1 -type f -print0 2>/dev/null)
        [[ ${#NEW_FILES[@]} -gt 0 ]] && break
        sleep 1
    done

    if [[ ${#NEW_FILES[@]} -eq 0 ]]; then
        echo "[assemble] ERROR: No new files"
        exit 1
    fi

    > "$AI_OUTPUT"
    for f in "${NEW_FILES[@]}"; do
        NAME=$(basename "$f")
        printf '//===== FILE: %s =====\n' "$NAME" >> "$AI_OUTPUT"
        cat "$f" >> "$AI_OUTPUT"
        printf '\n\n' >> "$AI_OUTPUT"
    done

    touch "$ASSEMBLED_FLAG"
    rm -f "$SNAPSHOT_FILE"
    echo "[assemble] DONE"
    exit 0
fi

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# MODE: normal build
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

# Stale state cleanup — always before a new build
echo "[cleanup] Removing stale flags and error logs"
rm -f "$COMPLETE_FLAG"
rm -f "$STATUS_FILE"
rm -rf "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"

echo "[normal] Starting build mode"
cd "$REPO_DIR"

# Clean old error logs from repo before reset to prevent re-detection
echo "[cleanup] Removing old build_error_logs from repo"
rm -rf "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs"

echo "[sync] Force syncing with origin/main"
git fetch origin main
git reset --hard origin/main
echo "[sync] Repo synced"

echo "[copy] Updating ai-output.txt"
cp "$AI_OUTPUT" "$REPO_DIR/ai-output.txt"

git config user.name  "AutoBuild Bot"
git config user.email "bot@autobuild.local"

git add ai-output.txt
git commit -m "AutoBuild: update ai-output.txt" || echo "[skip] Nothing to commit"
git push origin main || echo "[warn] git push failed"

echo "[wait] Waiting 20s for workflows to queue..."
sleep 20

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# Watch APK workflow
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
APK_WORKFLOW_NAME="Build APK"
CONCLUSION=""

echo "[watch] Looking for APK workflow run..."
APK_RUN_ID=$(gh run list \
    --workflow="$APK_WORKFLOW_NAME" \
    --limit=1 \
    --json databaseId \
    -q '.[0].databaseId' 2>/dev/null || true)

if [[ -z "${APK_RUN_ID:-}" ]]; then
    echo "[warn] No APK workflow run found — writing FAILURE"
    echo "FAILURE" > "$STATUS_FILE"
    touch "$COMPLETE_FLAG"
    echo "=== build_runner.sh DONE (no run found) $(date) ==="
    exit 0
fi

echo "[watch] Watching run $APK_RUN_ID..."
gh run watch "$APK_RUN_ID" --exit-status || true

# Deterministic result via gh run view
echo "[status] Querying conclusion for run $APK_RUN_ID..."
CONCLUSION=$(gh run view "$APK_RUN_ID" \
    --json conclusion \
    -q '.conclusion' 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
echo "[status] Conclusion = $CONCLUSION"

# Final sync to fetch any committed error logs
echo "[sync] Final git pull"
git fetch origin main
git reset --hard origin/main

# Write build_status.txt and handle logs
if [[ "$CONCLUSION" == "success" ]]; then
    echo "[result] BUILD SUCCESS"
    echo "SUCCESS" > "$STATUS_FILE"
    rm -rf "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
    mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
    echo "[result] Cleared error logs from shared storage"
else
    echo "[result] BUILD FAILURE (conclusion=$CONCLUSION)"
    echo "FAILURE" > "$STATUS_FILE"

    if [[ -d "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs" ]] && \
       [[ -f "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs/error_summary.txt" ]]; then
        rm -rf "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
        mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
        cp -f "$REPO_DIR/build_error_logs/"* "$ERROR_LOG_DIR/" 2>/dev/null || true
        echo "[result] Error logs copied to $ERROR_LOG_DIR"
    else
        echo "[warn] FAILURE but no error_summary.txt found in repo"
        mkdir -p "$ERROR_LOG_DIR"
        echo "Build failed but no error_summary.txt was committed." \
            > "$ERROR_LOG_DIR/error_summary.txt"
        echo "(gh conclusion=$CONCLUSION, no log files found)" \
            >> "$ERROR_LOG_DIR/error_summary.txt"
    fi
fi

# Always touch build_complete.flag last
echo "[final] Touching build_complete.flag"
touch "$COMPLETE_FLAG" || true

echo "=== build_runner.sh DONE (conclusion=$CONCLUSION) $(date) ==="

//===== TERMUXFILE: workflows/jarvis_start.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# ================================================================
#  jarvis_start.sh  —  Minimal Phone A startup
#  Only starts what is essential for the A→B agent loop:
#    1. ADB connect Phone A + Phone B
#    2. Verify Phone B Claude bridge is reachable
#
#  Phone A : 192.168.29.48:37891
#  Phone B : 192.168.29.110:45999  (Claude brain)
#
#  Usage:
#    bash ~/workflows/jarvis_start.sh
#    bash ~/workflows/jarvis_start.sh --stop
# ================================================================

PHONE_A="192.168.29.48:37891"
PHONE_B="192.168.29.110:45999"
PHONE_B_BRIDGE="http://192.168.29.110:8890"

GREEN="\033[0;32m"; YELLOW="\033[1;33m"; RED="\033[0;31m"; NC="\033[0m"
log()  { echo -e "${GREEN}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }
warn() { echo -e "${YELLOW}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }
err()  { echo -e "${RED}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }

# ── Stop mode ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [ "$1" = "--stop" ]; then
    log "Disconnecting ADB devices..."
    adb disconnect "$PHONE_A" 2>/dev/null && log "  ✓ Phone A disconnected" || true
    adb disconnect "$PHONE_B" 2>/dev/null && log "  ✓ Phone B disconnected" || true
    log "Done."; exit 0
fi

echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║   JARVIS START  —  Agent Loop (A → B)               ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""

# ── 1. ADB connect ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Connecting ADB devices..."

adb connect "$PHONE_A" 2>&1 | grep -q "connected" \
    && log "  ✓ Phone A ($PHONE_A)" \
    || warn "  ✗ Phone A failed — screencap will fail"

adb connect "$PHONE_B" 2>&1 | grep -q "connected" \
    && log "  ✓ Phone B ($PHONE_B)" \
    || warn "  ✗ Phone B failed — bridge unreachable"

# ── 2. Verify Phone B bridge ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Checking Phone B Claude bridge..."
HEALTH=$(curl -sf --max-time 5 "$PHONE_B_BRIDGE/health")
if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
    log "  ✓ Bridge online — Claude brain ACTIVE"
    log "  $HEALTH"
else
    err "  ✗ Bridge offline!"
    err "  On Phone B run: python3 ~/claude_bridge.py"
    echo ""
    exit 1
fi

# ── 3. Quick A→B smoke test ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Running A→B smoke test..."
RESULT=$(curl -sf --max-time 30 -X POST "$PHONE_B_BRIDGE/chat" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -d '{"prompt": "Reply with only the word: ready"}')
if echo "$RESULT" | grep -q '"success":true'; then
    log "  ✓ A→B round-trip OK"
    log "  Response: $RESULT"
else
    warn "  ✗ Smoke test failed or timed out"
    warn "  Raw: $RESULT"
fi

# ── Summary ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║   READY                                              ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""
log "Phone A (agent)  : $PHONE_A"
log "Phone B (brain)  : $PHONE_B_BRIDGE"
echo ""
log "Run agent:"
log "  cd ~/workflows"
log "  python3 test/jarvis-agent/agent/controller.py --task 'Open WhatsApp' --device '$PHONE_A'"
echo ""


//===== TERMUXFILE: workflows/claude_bridge.py =====
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
claude_bridge.py  —  Phone B Termux server
Samsung Galaxy A10s  —  720x1520

Session 6: OPT-4 v2 — bridge is now fully stateless.

All bypass decisions are made on Phone A (controller + llm_client).
Prompts that reach this bridge always go to Claude — no bypass logic here.

All Session 2/3/4 optimizations (OPT 1/2/3) preserved.

Session 10 fix:
  POLL_INTERVAL 0.7 → 0.4s, STABLE_COUNT 2 → 1.
  Claude response is already complete when Stop button disappears.
  One stable read is sufficient — saves 0.7-1.4s per Claude call.
"""

import base64
import json
import subprocess
import time
import re
from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
from pathlib import Path

PORT             = 8890
CLAUDE_PKG       = "com.anthropic.claude"
CLAUDE_ACTIVITY  = "com.anthropic.claude/.mainactivity.MainActivity"
POLL_INTERVAL    = 0.4   # was 0.7 — tighter poll, less wait after Claude finishes
STABLE_COUNT     = 1     # was 2 — one stable read is enough after Stop disappears
MAX_WAIT         = 120
SCREEN_W         = 720
SCREEN_H         = 1520

ADB    = "/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/adb"
SERIAL = "192.168.29.110:39991"   # <- Phone B confirmed port

USE_CLIPBOARD = True
PROMPT_TMP    = "/sdcard/.jv_prompt.txt"

LOG_DIR = Path.home() / ".jarvis_logs"
LOG_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)

# -- ADB helpers ---------------------------------------------------------------

def adb(*args, timeout=20) -> subprocess.CompletedProcess:
    cmd = [ADB, "-s", SERIAL] + list(str(a) for a in args)
    return subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, timeout=timeout)

def shell(*args, timeout=20) -> str:
    r = adb("shell", *args, timeout=timeout)
    return r.stdout.decode(errors="ignore").strip()

def ui_dump() -> str:
    shell("uiautomator", "dump", "/sdcard/uidump.xml")
    r = adb("shell", "cat", "/sdcard/uidump.xml", timeout=10)
    return r.stdout.decode(errors="ignore")

def tap(x, y):
    print(f"[tap] {x},{y}")
    shell("input", "tap", str(x), str(y))
    time.sleep(0.5)

def keyevent(code):
    shell("input", "keyevent", str(code))
    time.sleep(0.3)

# -- Clipboard paste (OPT 1) ---------------------------------------------------

def paste_via_clipper(text: str):
    print(f"[bridge] clipboard paste ({len(text)} chars)...")
    encoded = base64.b64encode(text.encode("utf-8")).decode("ascii")
    write_cmd = f"echo '{encoded}' | base64 -d > {PROMPT_TMP}"
    result = adb("shell", write_cmd)
    if result.returncode != 0:
        print(f"[bridge] WARNING: file write failed: {result.stderr.decode()}")
    time.sleep(0.15)
    clip_cmd = f"am broadcast -a clipper.set --es text \"$(cat {PROMPT_TMP})\""
    result = adb("shell", clip_cmd)
    out = result.stdout.decode(errors="ignore")
    print(f"[bridge] clipper set: {out.strip()[:80]}")
    time.sleep(0.3)
    shell("input", "keyevent", "279")
    time.sleep(0.2)
    print("[bridge] paste done")

# -- Word-by-word fallback -----------------------------------------------------

def adb_broadcast(text: str):
    subprocess.run([
        ADB, "-s", SERIAL,
        "shell", "am", "broadcast",
        "-a", "ADB_INPUT_TEXT",
        "--es", "msg", text
    ], capture_output=True, timeout=15)

def _sanitize_wordbyword(text: str) -> str:
    return (text
            .replace("'", "")
            .replace('"', "")
            .replace("\\", "")
            .replace("`", "")
            .replace("&", "and")
            .replace("|", " ")
            .replace(";", " ")
            .replace("\n", " "))

def type_text_wordbyword(text: str):
    safe  = _sanitize_wordbyword(text)
    words = safe.split(" ")
    total = len(words)
    print(f"[bridge] typing {total} words...")
    for i, word in enumerate(words):
        if word:
            adb_broadcast(word)
            time.sleep(0.1)
        if i < total - 1:
            shell("input", "keyevent", "62")
            time.sleep(0.05)
    print("[bridge] typing done")

def type_text(text: str):
    if USE_CLIPBOARD:
        paste_via_clipper(text)
    else:
        type_text_wordbyword(text)

# -- EditText detection --------------------------------------------------------

def find_edittext(xml: str):
    patterns = [
        r'class="android\.widget\.EditText"[^>]*bounds="\[(\d+),(\d+)\]\[(\d+),(\d+)\]"',
        r'class="android\.widget\.MultiAutoCompleteTextView"[^>]*bounds="\[(\d+),(\d+)\]\[(\d+),(\d+)\]"',
        r'class="com\.facebook\.react\.views\.textinput\.ReactEditText"[^>]*bounds="\[(\d+),(\d+)\]\[(\d+),(\d+)\]"',
        r'(?:hint-text="[^"]*[Mm]essage[^"]*"|content-desc="[^"]*[Mm]essage[^"]*")[^>]*bounds="\[(\d+),(\d+)\]\[(\d+),(\d+)\]"',
    ]
    for pat in patterns:
        m = re.search(pat, xml)
        if m:
            x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, m.groups())
            cx, cy = (x1 + x2) // 2, (y1 + y2) // 2
            print(f"[bridge] EditText found via pattern: class match, center=({cx},{cy})")
            return cx, cy
    for m in re.finditer(
        r'focusable="true"[^>]*bounds="\[(\d+),(\d+)\]\[(\d+),(\d+)\]"', xml
    ):
        x1, y1, x2, y2 = map(int, m.groups())
        cy = (y1 + y2) // 2
        if cy > SCREEN_H * 0.70:
            cx = (x1 + x2) // 2
            print(f"[bridge] EditText found via focusable fallback, center=({cx},{cy})")
            return cx, cy
    return None

def wait_for_input(timeout=30):
    print("[bridge] waiting for EditText...")
    for _ in range(timeout):
        xml = ui_dump()
        pos = find_edittext(xml)
        if pos:
            print(f"[bridge] EditText at {pos}")
            return pos
        time.sleep(1)
    return None

def type_prompt(text: str):
    shell("ime", "set", "com.android.adbkeyboard/.AdbIME")
    time.sleep(0.5)
    pos = wait_for_input()
    if not pos:
        print("[bridge] WARNING: no EditText found, using fallback (363,1235)")
        pos = (363, 1235)
    tap(*pos)
    time.sleep(0.5)
    keyevent("KEYCODE_CTRL_A")
    time.sleep(0.2)
    keyevent("KEYCODE_DEL")
    time.sleep(0.3)
    type_text(text)
    time.sleep(0.5)

# -- Claude app control (OPT 3) ------------------------------------------------

def _claude_is_foreground() -> bool:
    win_out = shell("dumpsys", "window", "windows")
    for line in win_out.splitlines():
        if ("mCurrentFocus" in line or "mFocusedApp" in line) and CLAUDE_PKG in line:
            return True
    act_out = shell("dumpsys", "activity", "activities")
    for line in act_out.splitlines():
        if "mResumedActivity" in line and CLAUDE_PKG in line:
            return True
    return False

def ensure_claude_foreground():
    if _claude_is_foreground():
        print("[bridge] Claude already foreground — skipping launch")
        return
    print("[bridge] Launching Claude...")
    subprocess.run([
        ADB, "-s", SERIAL,
        "shell", "am", "start",
        "-n", CLAUDE_ACTIVITY
    ], capture_output=True, timeout=10)
    for i in range(12):
        time.sleep(1)
        if _claude_is_foreground():
            print(f"[bridge] Claude foreground confirmed ({i+1}s)")
            return
        print(f"[bridge] waiting for Claude... ({i+1}s)")
    print("[bridge] WARNING: Claude foreground not confirmed after 12s, continuing...")
    time.sleep(1)

def tap_send():
    keyevent("66")
    time.sleep(1.5)

# -- Response extraction (OPT 2) -----------------------------------------------

SKIP_TEXTS = {
    "Send a message", "Message Claude", "New conversation",
    "Chat with Claude", "Chat with Claude\u2026", "Chat with Claude...",
    "How can I help you this morning?", "How can I help you today?",
    "How can I help you this afternoon?", "How can I help you this evening?",
    "Reply to Claude\u2026", "Reply to Claude...",
    "Get more with Claude Pro", "Upgrade", "Attach", "Add to chat",
    "Start speech input", "Voice Mode", "Toggle ghost mode",
    "Send", "Stop", "Retry",
    "Claude can make mistakes.", "Please double check responses.",
    "Please double-check responses.",
    "Claude is AI and can make mistakes.",
    "Claude is AI and can make mistakes. Please double-check responses.",
    "Sonnet 4.6", "Sonnet 4.6\ufffd",
    "Today", "New chat", "Chats", "Projects", "Artifacts",
    "Recents", "Search Chats", "Select", "Open menu",
    "Close all", "Search", "PGDN", "PGUP", "ESC", "HOME", "END",
}

SKIP_PREFIXES = (
    "You are a mobile", "You are an Android", "Your job:",
    "TASK:", "SCREEN", "HISTORY", "ACTION",
    "Available Actions", "Navigation Strategy",
    "Output ONLY", "Choose ONE", "RECENT ACTIONS", "WARNING:",
    "It looks like", "Is this a test", "Parsing this",
    "Sonnet", "Get more", "How can I help",
    "Please double-check", "Claude is AI",
)

def is_still_generating(dump_xml: str) -> bool:
    return 'content-desc="Stop"' in dump_xml or "Stop generating" in dump_xml

def extract_last_response(dump_xml: str) -> str:
    texts = re.findall(r'text="([^"]{3,})"', dump_xml)
    candidates = [
        t for t in texts
        if t not in SKIP_TEXTS
        and not any(t.startswith(p) for p in SKIP_PREFIXES)
        and not t.startswith("  ")
    ]
    return candidates[-1] if candidates else ""

def extract_action_from_response(full_text: str) -> str:
    lines = full_text.strip().splitlines()
    action_re = re.compile(
        r"^\s*(tap\s+\d+|tap\s+\d+[,x]\d+|type\s+.+|swipe\s+(up|down|left|right)"
        r"|back|home|enter|done)\s*$",
        re.I
    )
    for line in lines:
        if action_re.match(line.strip()):
            return line.strip()
    for line in reversed(lines):
        if line.strip():
            return line.strip()
    return full_text.strip()

def wait_for_response() -> str:
    print("[bridge] Waiting for response...")
    last_text = ""
    stable    = 0
    deadline  = time.time() + MAX_WAIT
    while time.time() < deadline:
        dump = ui_dump()
        if is_still_generating(dump):
            print("[bridge] ...generating...")
            stable = 0
            time.sleep(POLL_INTERVAL)
            continue
        current = extract_last_response(dump)
        if len(current) > len(last_text):
            last_text = current
            stable    = 0
            print(f"[bridge] Growing: {current[:60]!r}")
        elif current and current == last_text:
            stable += 1
            print(f"[bridge] Stable {stable}/{STABLE_COUNT}: {current[:60]!r}")
            if stable >= STABLE_COUNT:
                action = extract_action_from_response(current)
                print(f"[bridge] Done. Action: {action!r}")
                return action
        time.sleep(POLL_INTERVAL)
    print("[bridge] Timeout")
    return last_text or "home"

def get_claude_response(prompt: str) -> str:
    ensure_claude_foreground()
    time.sleep(1)
    type_prompt(prompt)
    tap_send()
    return wait_for_response()

def handle_prompt(prompt: str) -> dict:
    """All prompts that reach the bridge go straight to Claude."""
    response = get_claude_response(prompt)
    return {"response": response, "bypassed": False}

# -- HTTP server ---------------------------------------------------------------

class BridgeHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):

    def log_message(self, fmt, *args):
        print(f"[bridge] {fmt % args}")

    def send_json(self, code, data):
        body = json.dumps(data).encode()
        self.send_response(code)
        self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json")
        self.send_header("Access-Control-Allow-Origin", "*")
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(body)

    def do_GET(self):
        if self.path == "/health":
            self.send_json(200, {"success": True, "service": "claude_bridge",
                                 "screen": f"{SCREEN_W}x{SCREEN_H}",
                                 "serial": SERIAL,
                                 "opt4": "phone_a_side"})
        else:
            self.send_json(404, {"error": "not found"})

    def do_POST(self):
        length = int(self.headers.get("Content-Length", 0))
        body   = self.rfile.read(length)
        try:
            data = json.loads(body.decode())
        except Exception:
            self.send_json(400, {"success": False, "error": "invalid JSON"})
            return

        if self.path == "/chat":
            prompt = data.get("prompt", "").strip()
            if not prompt:
                self.send_json(400, {"success": False, "error": "missing prompt"})
                return
            print(f"\n[bridge] == PROMPT ==\n{prompt[:300]}\n{'='*40}")
            try:
                result = handle_prompt(prompt)
                print(f"[bridge] == ACTION ==\n{result}\n{'='*40}\n")
                self.send_json(200, {"success": True, **result})
            except Exception as e:
                import traceback
                traceback.print_exc()
                self.send_json(500, {"success": False, "error": str(e)})
        else:
            self.send_json(404, {"error": "not found"})

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗")
    print("║  JARVIS CLAUDE BRIDGE  —  Phone B (Galaxy A10s)     ║")
    print("╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝")
    print(f"  Screen  : {SCREEN_W}x{SCREEN_H}")
    print(f"  Port    : {PORT}")
    print(f"  Serial  : {SERIAL}")
    print(f"  ADB     : {ADB}")
    print(f"  Typing  : {'Clipper file-based (OPT 1)' if USE_CLIPBOARD else 'word-by-word (fallback)'}")
    print(f"  Poll    : {POLL_INTERVAL}s  Stable: {STABLE_COUNT}x  (Session 10)")
    print(f"  OPT 4   : bypass handled by Phone A — bridge is stateless")
    print()
    server = HTTPServer(("0.0.0.0", PORT), BridgeHandler)
    try:
        server.serve_forever()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n[bridge] Stopped.")
        server.shutdown()


//===== TERMUXFILE: test/jarvis_server_init.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# =====================================================================================================
#  jarvis_server_init.sh
#  Starts the complete JARVIS LLM server stack:
#    1. llamafile model server  (port 8080)
#    2. llamafile_proxy.py      (port 8888, no-auth — for agent)
#    3. llamafile_proxy_lan.py  (port 8889, LAN+auth — for Android app)
#
#  Usage:
#    bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh          # start all
#    bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh --pair   # start + enable LAN pairing
#    bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh --stop   # kill all
# =====================================================================================================

MODEL="$HOME/ai-workspace/llama.cpp/models/Qwen2.5-Coder-3B-Instruct-Q4_K_M.gguf"
LLAMAFILE="$HOME/llamafile"
PROXY_LOCAL="$HOME/llamafile_proxy.py"
PROXY_LAN="$HOME/llamafile_proxy_lan.py"

LOG_DIR="$HOME/.jarvis_logs"
mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"

GREEN="\033[0;32m"; YELLOW="\033[1;33m"; RED="\033[0;31m"; NC="\033[0m"
log()  { echo -e "${GREEN}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }
warn() { echo -e "${YELLOW}[jarvis]${NC} $*"; }

# ── Stop mode ────────────────────────────────────────────────
if [ "$1" = "--stop" ]; then
    log "Stopping all JARVIS processes..."
    pkill -f "llamafile" 2>/dev/null && log "  ✓ llamafile stopped" || true
    pkill -f "llamafile_proxy" 2>/dev/null && log "  ✓ proxies stopped" || true
    log "Done."
    exit 0
fi

# ── Pre-flight checks ────────────────────────────────────────
echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║   🚀 JARVIS SERVER INIT                              ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""

[ -f "$LLAMAFILE" ] || { echo -e "${RED}[error]${NC} llamafile not found at $LLAMAFILE"; echo "Run: bash ~/jarvis_setup.sh"; exit 1; }
[ -f "$MODEL" ]     || { warn "Model not found: $MODEL"; warn "Agent will fall back to subprocess mode"; }
[ -f "$PROXY_LOCAL" ] || { warn "llamafile_proxy.py not found at $PROXY_LOCAL"; }
[ -f "$PROXY_LAN" ]   || { warn "llamafile_proxy_lan.py not found at $PROXY_LAN"; }

# ── Kill stale processes ─────────────────────────────────────
log "Cleaning up stale processes..."
pkill -f "llamafile" 2>/dev/null || true
pkill -f "llamafile_proxy" 2>/dev/null || true
sleep 1

# ── 1. Start llamafile server ────────────────────────────────
if [ -f "$MODEL" ]; then
    log "Starting llamafile server (port 8080)..."
    nohup "$LLAMAFILE" -m "$MODEL" \
        --server --port 8080 --host 127.0.0.1 \
        --ctx-size 4096 --threads 4 \
        --n-predict 256 \
        --log-disable \
        > "$LOG_DIR/llamafile.log" 2>&1 &
    LLAMAFILE_PID=$!
    log "  PID: $LLAMAFILE_PID — waiting for model to load..."

    # Wait up to 60s for server to become ready
    READY=0
    for i in $(seq 1 30); do
        sleep 2
        if curl -sf "http://127.0.0.1:8080/health" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
            log "  ✓ llamafile ready after ${i}×2s"
            READY=1; break
        fi
        printf "."
    done
    echo ""
    [ $READY -eq 1 ] || warn "llamafile may still be loading — proxy will retry"
else
    warn "Skipping llamafile (model missing)"
fi

# ── 2. Start local proxy (port 8888) ────────────────────────
if [ -f "$PROXY_LOCAL" ]; then
    log "Starting local proxy (port 8888)..."
    nohup python3 "$PROXY_LOCAL" \
        > "$LOG_DIR/proxy_local.log" 2>&1 &
    PROXY_PID=$!
    sleep 1
    if curl -sf "http://127.0.0.1:8888/health" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        log "  ✓ local proxy ready (PID $PROXY_PID)"
    else
        warn "  proxy may still be starting — check $LOG_DIR/proxy_local.log"
    fi
fi

# ── 3. Start LAN proxy (port 8889) ───────────────────────────
if [ -f "$PROXY_LAN" ]; then
    log "Starting LAN proxy (port 8889)..."
    PAIR_FLAG=""
    [ "$1" = "--pair" ] && PAIR_FLAG="--pair --duration 300"
    nohup python3 "$PROXY_LAN" $PAIR_FLAG \
        > "$LOG_DIR/proxy_lan.log" 2>&1 &
    LAN_PID=$!
    sleep 1
    if curl -sf "http://127.0.0.1:8889/health" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
        log "  ✓ LAN proxy ready (PID $LAN_PID)"
    else
        warn "  LAN proxy starting — check $LOG_DIR/proxy_lan.log"
    fi
fi

# ── Summary ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║  ✅  JARVIS SERVER STACK RUNNING                     ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""
log "Endpoints:"
log "  llamafile  : http://127.0.0.1:8080  (OpenAI-compat)"
log "  proxy      : http://127.0.0.1:8888  (agent, no-auth)"
log "  LAN proxy  : http://127.0.0.1:8889  (Android app, auth)"
echo ""
log "Logs: $LOG_DIR/"
echo ""
log "Test:"
log "  curl -s http://127.0.0.1:8888/health"
log "  curl -X POST http://127.0.0.1:8888/chat_sync -H 'Content-Type: application/json' -d '{\"query\":\"hello\"}'"
echo ""
[ "$1" = "--pair" ] && log "⚡ Pairing mode ON for 5 minutes — pair from Android app now"
echo ""


//===== TERMUXFILE: test/jarvis_setup.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# =====================================================================================================
#  jarvis_setup.sh  — Full Jarvis Agent + Server Setup
#  Run ONCE in Termux.
#
#  What this does:
#    1. Install packages (python, android-tools, inotify-tools, wget)
#    2. Download llamafile binary (if missing)
#    3. Connect ADB to device
#    4. Create /sdcard/jarvis/ IPC directory
#    5. Deploy all Python agent files
#    6. Deploy server scripts (jarvis_server_init.sh, proxies, executor)
#    7. Smoke-test imports
#
#  After setup, start the system:
#    bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh      # starts llamafile + proxy
#    bash ~/jarvis_executor.sh &       # starts file IPC daemon
#    cd ~/jarvis-agent && python agent/controller.py
# =====================================================================================================

set -e

AGENT_DIR="$HOME/jarvis-agent"
WORKSPACE="$HOME/ai-workspace"
MODEL_DIR="$WORKSPACE/llama.cpp/models"
JARVIS_IPC="/sdcard/jarvis"
ADB_DEVICE="192.168.29.48:39935"
LLAMAFILE_BIN="$HOME/llamafile"
LLAMAFILE_URL="https://github.com/Mozilla-Ocho/llamafile/releases/download/0.8.13/llamafile-0.8.13"

GREEN="\033[0;32m"; YELLOW="\033[1;33m"; RED="\033[0;31m"; NC="\033[0m"
log()  { echo -e "${GREEN}[setup]${NC} $*"; }
warn() { echo -e "${YELLOW}[warn]${NC}  $*"; }
err()  { echo -e "${RED}[error]${NC} $*"; exit 1; }

echo ""
echo "╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║     JARVIS FULL SYSTEM SETUP                     ║"
echo "╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""

# ── 1. Packages ──────────────────────────────────────────
log "Installing packages..."
pkg update -y -q
pkg install -y python android-tools inotify-tools wget curl
pip install --quiet requests pillow
log "✓ Packages ready"

# ── 2. llamafile binary ──────────────────────────────────
if [ -f "$LLAMAFILE_BIN" ]; then
    log "✓ llamafile already present"
else
    log "Downloading llamafile..."
    wget -q --show-progress -O "$LLAMAFILE_BIN" "$LLAMAFILE_URL"
    chmod +x "$LLAMAFILE_BIN"
    log "✓ llamafile downloaded"
fi

# Add llamafile to PATH for this session
export PATH="$HOME:$PATH"

# ── 3. ADB ───────────────────────────────────────────────
log "Connecting ADB to $ADB_DEVICE ..."
adb connect "$ADB_DEVICE" 2>&1 | grep -q "connected" && log "✓ ADB connected" \
    || warn "ADB connect may have failed — check device IP"

# ── 4. IPC directory ─────────────────────────────────────
log "Creating IPC dir at $JARVIS_IPC ..."
mkdir -p "$JARVIS_IPC"
chmod 777 "$JARVIS_IPC" 2>/dev/null || true
touch "$JARVIS_IPC/command.txt" "$JARVIS_IPC/result.txt"
chmod 666 "$JARVIS_IPC/command.txt" "$JARVIS_IPC/result.txt" 2>/dev/null || true
echo "ready" > "$JARVIS_IPC/status.txt"
log "✓ IPC dir ready"

# ── 5. Create model dir ──────────────────────────────────
mkdir -p "$MODEL_DIR"
MODEL_FILE="$MODEL_DIR/Qwen2.5-Coder-3B-Instruct-Q4_K_M.gguf"
if [ -f "$MODEL_FILE" ]; then
    SIZE=$(du -sh "$MODEL_FILE" | cut -f1)
    log "✓ Model found ($SIZE)"
else
    warn "Model not found: $MODEL_FILE"
    warn "Download it:"
    warn "  cd $MODEL_DIR"
    warn "  wget https://huggingface.co/Qwen/Qwen2.5-Coder-3B-Instruct-GGUF/resolve/main/qwen2.5-coder-3b-instruct-q4_k_m.gguf"
fi

# ─ agent/state.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/agent/state.py" << 'PYEOF'
from dataclasses import dataclass, field

@dataclass
class AgentState:
    task: str
    step: int = 0
    history: list = field(default_factory=list)
    last_screen: str = ""
    last_ui: list = field(default_factory=list)
    done: bool = False
    max_steps: int = 20

    def record(self, action: dict, ui_elements: list) -> None:
        act = action.get("action", "?")
        if act == "tap":
            tid = action.get("target")
            label = next((e["text"] for e in ui_elements if e["id"] == tid), f"id={tid}")
            self.history.append(f"tap [{tid}] {label}")
        else:
            self.history.append(act)
        self.step += 1

    def is_finished(self) -> bool:
        return self.done or self.step >= self.max_steps

    def summary(self) -> str:
        return f"Task: {self.task} | Step: {self.step}/{self.max_steps} | History: {self.history}"
PYEOF

# ─ agent/controller.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/agent/controller.py" << 'PYEOF'
import sys, os, time, argparse

ROOT = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
sys.path.insert(0, ROOT)

from perception.screen_capture import capture_screen
from perception.ui_mock_parser  import parse_ui
from reasoning.prompt_builder   import build_prompt
from reasoning.llm_client       import generate, health_check
from reasoning.action_parser    import parse_action
from executor.adb_executor      import execute
from agent.state                import AgentState

DEFAULT_DEVICE = "192.168.29.48:39935"
DEFAULT_TASK   = "Open WhatsApp"
DEFAULT_MODEL  = os.path.expanduser(
    "~/ai-workspace/llama.cpp/models/Qwen2.5-Coder-3B-Instruct-Q4_K_M.gguf"
)
LOOP_SLEEP_SEC = 1.5

def run_step(state, device, model_path):
    print(f"\n{'='*55}\n  STEP {state.step+1}  |  {state.task}\n{'='*55}")
    img_path = capture_screen(adb_device=device)
    state.last_screen = img_path
    ui = parse_ui(img_path)
    state.last_ui = ui
    prompt = build_prompt(state.task, ui, history=state.history)
    llm_output = generate(prompt, model_path=model_path)
    print(f"[step] LLM decision: {llm_output!r}")
    action = parse_action(llm_output)
    print(f"[step] Parsed action: {action}")
    execute(action, ui, adb_device=device)
    state.record(action, ui)
    if action.get("action") == "done":
        state.done = True
    print(f"[step] {state.summary()}")

def run(task, device, model_path, max_steps=20):
    print(f"\n{'#'*55}")
    print(f"  JARVIS AGENT  —  {task}")
    print(f"  Device : {device}")
    print(f"  Model  : {os.path.basename(model_path)}")
    print(f"{'#'*55}\n")

    hc = health_check()
    print(f"[init] LLM backends: {hc}")
    if not any([hc["proxy"], hc["llamafile"], hc["binary"]]):
        print("[init] ⚠ WARNING: No LLM backend available. Start: bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh")

    state = AgentState(task=task, max_steps=max_steps)
    while not state.is_finished():
        try:
            run_step(state, device=device, model_path=model_path)
        except KeyboardInterrupt:
            print("\n[controller] Interrupted."); break
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[controller] Step error: {e}\nRetrying in 3s...")
            time.sleep(3); state.step += 1; continue
        if state.done:
            print(f"\n[controller] ✓ Task complete in {state.step} steps."); break
        time.sleep(LOOP_SLEEP_SEC)

    print(f"\n[controller] Final history:")
    for i, h in enumerate(state.history, 1):
        print(f"  {i}. {h}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Jarvis Agent Controller")
    p.add_argument("--task",      default=DEFAULT_TASK)
    p.add_argument("--device",    default=DEFAULT_DEVICE)
    p.add_argument("--model",     default=DEFAULT_MODEL)
    p.add_argument("--max-steps", default=20, type=int)
    args = p.parse_args()
    run(args.task, args.device, args.model, args.max_steps)
PYEOF

# ─ perception/__init__.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/perception/__init__.py" << 'PYEOF'

# ─ perception/screen_capture.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/perception/screen_capture.py" << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, os

LOCAL_PATH = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), "..", "screen.png")

def capture_screen(adb_device: str, local_path: str = LOCAL_PATH) -> str:
    local_path = os.path.abspath(local_path)
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["adb", "-s", adb_device, "exec-out", "screencap", "-p"],
        capture_output=True, timeout=15
    )
    if result.returncode != 0:
        raise RuntimeError(f"screencap failed: {result.stderr.decode().strip()}")
    if len(result.stdout) < 100:
        raise RuntimeError("screencap returned empty data")
    with open(local_path, "wb") as f:
        f.write(result.stdout)
    print(f"[capture] Screenshot saved ({len(result.stdout)} bytes)")
    return local_path
PYEOF

MOCK_ELEMENTS = [
    {"id": 1, "text": "WhatsApp",  "x": 160,  "y": 1200},
    {"id": 2, "text": "Chrome",    "x": 480,  "y": 1200},

    {"id": 7, "text": "Search",    "x": 540,  "y": 200},

# ─ reasoning/prompt_builder.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/reasoning/prompt_builder.py" << 'PYEOF'
SYSTEM_HEADER = "You are an Android control agent.\nChoose ONE action. Reply with ONLY the action. No explanation."
ACTION_MENU = "Actions:\n  tap <id>\n  back\n  home\n  done"

def build_prompt(task: str, ui_elements: list, history: list = None) -> str:
    lines = [SYSTEM_HEADER, "", f"TASK: {task}", "", "SCREEN:"]
    for el in ui_elements:
        lines.append(f"  [{el['id']}] {el['text']}")
    if history:
        lines += ["", "DONE SO FAR:"] + [f"  {h}" for h in history[-4:]]
    lines += ["", ACTION_MENU, "", "Your action:"]
    return "\n".join(lines)
PYEOF

# ─ reasoning/llm_client.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/reasoning/llm_client.py" << 'PYEOF'
import json, os, subprocess, shutil, urllib.request

PROXY_URL     = "http://127.0.0.1:8888"
LLAMAFILE_URL = "http://127.0.0.1:8080"
DEFAULT_MODEL = os.path.expanduser("~/ai-workspace/llama.cpp/models/Qwen2.5-Coder-3B-Instruct-Q4_K_M.gguf")
LLAMA_BINS    = ["llama-cli", "llama-simple-chat", "llamafile", "main"]

def _post(url, payload, timeout=60):
    body = json.dumps(payload).encode()
    req = urllib.request.Request(url, data=body, headers={"Content-Type":"application/json"}, method="POST")
    with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=timeout) as r:
        return json.loads(r.read().decode())

def _ok(url, t=3):
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=t) as r: return r.status == 200
    except: return False

def generate(prompt, model_path=DEFAULT_MODEL, max_tokens=64, temperature=0.1, timeout=60):
    print(f"[llm] Generating... tail: ...{prompt[-80:].strip()!r}")

    if _ok(f"{PROXY_URL}/health"):
        try:
            d = _post(f"{PROXY_URL}/chat_sync", {"query": prompt}, timeout=timeout)
            if d.get("success"):
                out = (d.get("response") or "").strip()
                print(f"[llm] ✓ proxy: {out!r}"); return out
        except Exception as e: print(f"[llm] proxy err: {e}")

    if _ok(f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/health"):
        try:
            d = _post(f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/v1/chat/completions",
                      {"messages":[{"role":"user","content":prompt}],
                       "max_tokens":max_tokens,"temperature":temperature}, timeout=timeout)
            out = d["choices"][0]["message"]["content"].strip()
            print(f"[llm] ✓ llamafile: {out!r}"); return out
        except Exception as e: print(f"[llm] llamafile err: {e}")

    mp = os.path.expanduser(model_path)
    binary = next((shutil.which(b) for b in LLAMA_BINS if shutil.which(b)), None)
    if not binary or not os.path.isfile(mp):
        raise RuntimeError("No LLM backend. Run: bash ~/jarvis_server_init.sh")
    r = subprocess.run([binary,"-m",mp,"-p",prompt,"-n",str(max_tokens),
                        "--temp",str(temperature),"--no-display-prompt","-e","--log-disable"],
                       capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout)
    out = "\n".join(l for l in r.stdout.strip().splitlines()
                    if not l.startswith("llama") and not l.startswith("[")).strip()
    print(f"[llm] ✓ subprocess: {out!r}"); return out

def health_check():
    return {"proxy":_ok(f"{PROXY_URL}/health"), "llamafile":_ok(f"{LLAMAFILE_URL}/health"),
            "binary":next((shutil.which(b) for b in LLAMA_BINS if shutil.which(b)),None)}
PYEOF

# ─ reasoning/action_parser.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/reasoning/action_parser.py" << 'PYEOF'
import re
_TAP  = re.compile(r"\btap\s+(\d+)", re.I)
_BACK = re.compile(r"\bback\b", re.I)
_HOME = re.compile(r"\bhome\b", re.I)
_DONE = re.compile(r"\bdone\b", re.I)

def parse_action(text: str) -> dict:
    if not text or not text.strip():
        return {"action": "home"}
    for line in text.splitlines():
        m = _TAP.search(line)
        if m: return {"action":"tap","target":int(m.group(1))}
        if _BACK.search(line): return {"action":"back"}
        if _HOME.search(line): return {"action":"home"}
        if _DONE.search(line): return {"action":"done"}
    print(f"[parser] unrecognised: {text!r} → home")
    return {"action": "home"}
PYEOF

# ─ executor/__init__.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/executor/__init__.py" << 'PYEOF'
PYEOF

# ─ executor/adb_executor.py ─
cat > "$AGENT_DIR/executor/adb_executor.py" << 'PYEOF'
import subprocess, time

def _adb(device, *args, timeout=10):
    cmd = ["adb", "-s", device] + list(args)
    print(f"[adb] {' '.join(cmd)}")
    return subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout)

def execute(action: dict, ui_elements: list, adb_device: str) -> bool:
    act = action.get("action", "").lower()
    if act == "tap":
        tid = action.get("target")
        el = next((e for e in ui_elements if e["id"] == tid), None)
        if not el: print(f"[executor] element {tid} not found"); return False
        print(f"[executor] Tapping [{tid}] {el['text']} at ({el['x']},{el['y']})")
        _adb(adb_device, "shell", "input", "tap", str(el["x"]), str(el["y"]))
        time.sleep(0.5); return True
    elif act == "back":
        _adb(adb_device, "shell", "input", "keyevent", "4"); time.sleep(0.3); return True
    elif act == "home":
        _adb(adb_device, "shell", "input", "keyevent", "3"); time.sleep(0.3); return True
    elif act == "done":
        return False
    print(f"[executor] unknown action: {act!r}"); return False
PYEOF

log "✓ Agent files deployed"

log "Deploying server scripts..."

# llamafile_server.sh — wrapper to launch model

if [ ! -f "\$MODEL" ]; then echo "Model not found: \$MODEL"; exit 1; fi
echo "Starting llamafile server on port 8080..."
\$HOME/llamafile -m "\$MODEL" --server --port 8080 --host 127.0.0.1 \
  --ctx-size 4096 --threads 4 --n-predict 256 --log-disable
SHEOF2
chmod +x "$HOME/llamafile_server.sh"
log "✓ llamafile_server.sh"

//===== TERMUXFILE: test/jarvis_executor.sh =====
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# OPTIMIZED JARVIS Command Executor Service
# ZERO-DELAY file-based execution using inotify
# NOW WITH: Non-interactive mode + Command timeout

# ==============================================================================================================================
# CONFIGURATION
# ==============================================================================================================================

WORK_DIR="/sdcard/jarvis"
COMMAND_FILE="$WORK_DIR/command.txt"
RESULT_FILE="$WORK_DIR/result.txt"
STATUS_FILE="$WORK_DIR/status.txt"
LOG_FILE="$WORK_DIR/executor.log"

# Command timeout in seconds (prevent hanging on interactive commands)
COMMAND_TIMEOUT=60

# ==============================================================================================================================
# SETUP
# ==============================================================================================================================

# Install inotify-tools if not present (for instant file monitoring)
if ! command -v inotifywait &> /dev/null; then
    echo "Installing inotify-tools for zero-delay execution..."
    pkg install -y inotify-tools
fi

# Create directory
mkdir -p "$WORK_DIR" || {
    echo "❌ Error: Cannot create directory $WORK_DIR"
    exit 1
}

# Set permissions
chmod 777 "$WORK_DIR" 2>/dev/null

# Clean up old files
rm -f "$COMMAND_FILE" "$RESULT_FILE" "$STATUS_FILE" 2>/dev/null

# Create empty files
touch "$COMMAND_FILE" "$RESULT_FILE" "$STATUS_FILE" 2>/dev/null
chmod 666 "$COMMAND_FILE" "$RESULT_FILE" "$STATUS_FILE" 2>/dev/null

# ==============================================================================================================================
# LOGGING FUNCTION
# ==============================================================================================================================

log() {
    local timestamp=$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
    local message="[$timestamp] $1"
    echo "$message"
    echo "$message" >> "$LOG_FILE" 2>/dev/null
}

# ==============================================================================================================================
# STARTUP MESSAGE
# ==============================================================================================================================

clear
echo "╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗"
echo "║       🚀 JARVIS Command Executor Service v3.1            ║"
echo "║    (NON-INTERACTIVE + TIMEOUT PROTECTION + INOTIFY)      ║"
echo "╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝"
echo ""
echo "📍 Working Directory: $WORK_DIR"
echo "📥 Command File: $COMMAND_FILE"
echo "📤 Result File: $RESULT_FILE"
echo "📊 Status File: $STATUS_FILE"
echo "📝 Log File: $LOG_FILE"
echo "⏱️  Command Timeout: ${COMMAND_TIMEOUT}s"
echo ""

# Verify files exist
if [ -f "$COMMAND_FILE" ] && [ -f "$RESULT_FILE" ]; then
    echo "✅ Communication files created successfully"
else
    echo "❌ ERROR: Failed to create communication files"
    exit 1
fi

# Write status
echo "ready" > "$STATUS_FILE"

echo ""
echo "⚡ Using inotify for instant command detection (NO POLLING!)"
echo "🔒 Non-interactive mode enabled (auto-yes for prompts)"
echo "⏱️  Timeout protection: ${COMMAND_TIMEOUT}s per command"
echo "🎧 Listening for commands from JARVIS app..."
echo "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━"
echo ""

log "JARVIS Executor v3.1 started (NON-INTERACTIVE + TIMEOUT mode)"

# ==============================================================================================================================
# COMMAND PROCESSING LOOP - ZERO DELAY WITH INOTIFY
# ==============================================================================================================================

# Trap to handle script termination
trap 'log "Executor stopped"; echo "stopped" > "$STATUS_FILE"; exit 0' INT TERM

# Command counter
CMD_COUNT=0
LAST_COMMAND=""

# Monitor file changes with inotify (instant detection, no polling!)
inotifywait -m -e modify,close_write "$COMMAND_FILE" 2>/dev/null | while read -r directory events filename
do
    # Read command immediately when file is modified
    if [ -f "$COMMAND_FILE" ] && [ -s "$COMMAND_FILE" ]; then
        command=$(cat "$COMMAND_FILE" 2>/dev/null | tr -d '\r\n')
        
        # Skip if empty or same as last command
        if [ -z "$command" ] || [ "$command" = "$LAST_COMMAND" ]; then
            continue
        fi
        
        LAST_COMMAND="$command"
        CMD_COUNT=$((CMD_COUNT + 1))
        
        # Update status
        echo "executing" > "$STATUS_FILE"
        
        # Log received command
        echo "━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━"
        echo "⚡ Command #$CMD_COUNT received INSTANTLY at $(date '+%H:%M:%S.%3N')"
        echo "   Command: $command"
        log "INSTANT execution #$CMD_COUNT: $command"
        
        # Execute command with timeout and non-interactive stdin
        # Key changes:
        # 1. Close stdin with </dev/null (prevents waiting for user input)
        # 2. Use 'yes' to auto-answer prompts
        # 3. Wrap in timeout command
        START_TIME=$(date +%s%3N)
        
        # Create a temporary script to execute with timeout
        temp_script=$(mktemp)
        cat > "$temp_script" << EOF
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# Auto-answer 'yes' to all prompts and execute command
yes | eval "$command" 2>&1
EOF
        chmod +x "$temp_script"
        
        # Execute with timeout (will kill after COMMAND_TIMEOUT seconds)
        if command -v timeout &> /dev/null; then
            # Use timeout if available
            output=$(timeout ${COMMAND_TIMEOUT}s bash "$temp_script" 2>&1)
            exit_code=$?
            
            # Check if timeout occurred (exit code 124)
            if [ $exit_code -eq 124 ]; then
                output="ERROR: Command timed out after ${COMMAND_TIMEOUT} seconds. This usually means:\n- Command is waiting for user input (use -y flags)\n- Command is stuck or taking too long\n\nOriginal output:\n$output"
                exit_code=124
            fi
        else
            # Fallback without timeout (not recommended but still better than hanging)
            output=$(bash "$temp_script" 2>&1)
            exit_code=$?
        fi
        
        # Clean up temp script
        rm -f "$temp_script"
        
        END_TIME=$(date +%s%3N)
        DURATION=$(( (END_TIME - START_TIME) ))
        
        # Write result to file IMMEDIATELY
        # Format: exit_code|output
        echo "$exit_code|$output" > "$RESULT_FILE"
        
        # Force sync to ensure file is written
        sync
        
        # Update status
        echo "ready" > "$STATUS_FILE"
        
        # Clear command file to be ready for next command
        echo "" > "$COMMAND_FILE"
        
        # Log completion
        if [ $exit_code -eq 0 ]; then
            echo "✅ Command completed in ${DURATION}ms"
            log "Command #$CMD_COUNT completed: exit=$exit_code, ${DURATION}ms"
        elif [ $exit_code -eq 124 ]; then
            echo "⏱️  Command TIMED OUT after ${COMMAND_TIMEOUT}s"
            log "Command #$CMD_COUNT TIMEOUT: ${COMMAND_TIMEOUT}s"
        else
            echo "❌ Command failed with exit code: $exit_code in ${DURATION}ms"
            log "Command #$CMD_COUNT failed: exit=$exit_code, ${DURATION}ms"
        fi
        
        # Show output preview (first 3 lines)
        if [ -n "$output" ]; then
            echo "   Output preview:"
            echo "$output" | head -3 | sed 's/^/   │ /'
            if [ $(echo "$output" | wc -l) -gt 3 ]; then
                echo "   │ ... ($(echo "$output" | wc -l) total lines)"
            fi
        fi
        echo ""
    fi
done

#!/bin/bash
# Use llamafile - a single executable that runs LLMs with built-in server

    echo "✅ llamafile already downloaded"

    chmod +x "$LLAMAFILE"
    echo "✅ Downloaded"
